## Security Audit Findings (2026-04-16) — shipped

- [x] SEC-DONE-1. **BH-S002 / LIVE-03 — `/super-admin/*` localhost-only guard.** Applied new `middleware/localhostOnly.ts` to `/super-admin/api` mount and both `/super-admin` HTML routes in `index.ts`. Guard checks `req.socket.remoteAddress` (actual TCP source, not spoofable `req.ip`) against `127.0.0.1 / ::1 / ::ffff:127.0.0.1` and returns 404 (not 403) so endpoint existence isn't confirmed to non-local callers. Pre-fix: forged super-admin JWT + master.db session write → 200 full tenant list from anywhere on the internet. Post-fix: external probes against bizarrecrm.com return 404 for GET/POST; non-GET/POST return uniform 403 from CSRF middleware (no existence leak). Loopback preserved — operator RDP/SSH into prod host + browse https://127.0.0.1/super-admin still works. Reduces BH-S002 severity from HIGH (internet-reachable with host compromise) to LOW (operator-hygiene; exploit requires host compromise which already = game over). Commit `585a06c` on main. Verified live against bizarrecrm.com:
  - GET `/super-admin/api/tenants` from external → 404 `{"success":false,"message":"Not found"}` (was 401)
  - GET `/super-admin` HTML from external → 404 (was 200 login page)
  - POST `/super-admin/api/auth/login` with Origin header from external → 404 (was reaching auth layer)
  - GET `/super-admin/api/tenants` from 127.0.0.1 on prod host → 401 (JWT gate reachable, as intended)
  - Non-local enumeration across 10 variant paths all returned 404 uniform

- [x] SEC-L43. **Audit log no longer persists attacker-supplied login input.** `auth.routes.ts:551` (unknown-user login path), `:576` (bad-password path), `:1128` (unknown-email forgot-password path) now log `<unknown-user>` in place of the raw POST body, or the canonical `user.username` resolved from the DB when a user was found. Prevents audit-log poisoning with arbitrary strings (ctrl chars, giant blobs, SQL-ish payloads) and stops leaking enumeration attempts back into long-lived event tables. IP + intent are still recorded so rate-limit/abuse detection is intact. (trace-login-006 / trace-reset-004)

- [x] SEC-L47. **Zero-dollar invoice reject guard.** `pos.routes.ts` `/transaction` endpoint now rejects invoices with `total === 0` unless the caller passes `allow_zero_dollar=1` (or `true` / `'1'`) AND the authenticated cashier has `admin` or `owner` role. The empty-cart case is still caught earlier at `items.length === 0`; this guard handles the "cart resolves to $0 after discount-stack / free-item" case that previously completed silently. Default POS sales are unaffected since non-zero totals short-circuit the check. (trace-pos-001)

- [x] SEC-M38. **Stripe webhook `constructEvent` explicit tolerance.** `services/stripe.ts:verifyWebhook` now passes an explicit 300-second (5 min) tolerance as the 4th positional argument (matches the SDK's `(payload, header, secret, tolerance?)` signature — the `{ tolerance: 300 }` object form suggested in the audit note is not supported by the current `stripe` npm package). Documented via a module-level `WEBHOOK_TOLERANCE_SECONDS` constant and a comment explaining that a drifting host clock will start failing verification intentionally. Default was already 300s but is now pinned so a future SDK default change can't silently widen the replay window. (PAY-06)

- [x] SEC-M39. **BlockChyp `getClient()` accepts pre-snapshotted config.** `services/blockchyp.ts:getClient` now takes an optional `cfgSnapshot?: BlockChypConfig` parameter; `processPayment` (the only caller holding an active snapshot) now passes its locked `cfgSnapshot` through so `getClient` doesn't re-read `store_config` a second time. Eliminates the tiny TOCTOU window where test-mode could flip between the caller's `getBlockChypConfig(db)` call and `getClient`'s own implicit read. Cache key still hashes the effective config so older callers that pass no snapshot keep today's behavior. (PAY-24)

- [x] SEC-M40. **Stripe `updateSubscription` proration_behavior pinned + configurable.** `services/stripe.ts` already passed `proration_behavior: 'create_prorations'` but it's now resolved through `resolveProrationBehavior()` so operators can override via `STRIPE_PRORATION_BEHAVIOR` env var (allowed: `create_prorations`, `none`, `always_invoice`). Unknown/typo values fall back to `create_prorations` so a misconfigured env var can't silently disable proration. (PAY-25)

- [x] SEC-M32. **forgot-password timing equalization.** `auth.routes.ts` `/forgot-password` now (a) captures `startNs` at entry, (b) always runs a dummy `bcrypt.compareSync` with a 12-round `$2b$12$` hash on the not-found path so CPU work matches the found-path sha256+UPDATE+SMTP cost, (c) detaches `sendEmail` via `void (async () => { ... })()` so SMTP latency can no longer leak the found/not-found bit, and (d) calls `enforceMinDuration(startNs, 500)` on both paths so observable response time is clamped to ≥500ms regardless. Email-delivery failures are still logged via `logger.warn` (same behavior as before), just no longer in the critical path. (trace-reset-003)

- [x] SEC-L46. **Membership renewal cron bumped to 100 per run + per-tenant timeout.** `index.ts` membership renewal cron: `MEMBERSHIP_MAX_PER_RUN` raised from 10 → 100 (shops with >10 active monthly memberships no longer accumulate debt faster than the cron can drain it). Added `MEMBERSHIP_PER_TENANT_TIMEOUT_MS = 10 * 60 * 1000` and wrapped each tenant's work unit in a `Promise.race` against a rejected timer — a hung BlockChyp call on one tenant can no longer stall the whole cron across all tenants. Extracted the per-tenant body into a nested `membershipTenantWork()` function; `chargeToken` lifted out of the try block so the nested function can see it. (REL-026)

- [x] SEC-L11. **metrics.db daily `PRAGMA incremental_vacuum(50)`.** `services/metricsCollector.ts` now sets `PRAGMA auto_vacuum = INCREMENTAL` on DB creation (takes effect on a brand-new metrics.db; existing DBs need a one-time VACUUM to activate — the incremental_vacuum call is a harmless no-op in that case). `rollupHourly` fires every hour and calls a new `maybeDailyVacuum(db)` helper that tracks `lastVacuumAt` in a module-local variable and runs `PRAGMA incremental_vacuum(50)` at most once per 24h. Restart-friendly (re-triggers on next tick after startup). (REL-036)

- [x] SEC-L41. **Slug-check captcha after 3 free calls per IP.** `signup.routes.ts` `/check-slug/:slug`: added an in-memory `slugCheckCounters` Map keyed by IP with a 1h sliding window. First 3 calls per IP behave exactly as before; subsequent calls require a hCaptcha token via `?captcha=<token>` or return 403 with `{ captcha_required: true }`. The counter only increments after the captcha gate passes, so a stuck client can't keep ratcheting the count up. Existing 5-min sweeper cadence reused for counter expiry. Stacks with existing `slugCheckLimiter` (1-per-10s) — rate limit hits first, captcha gate hits second. (trace-signup-005)

- [x] SEC-L45. **Collapse signup step-specific error messages into generic reference-id message.** `services/tenant-provisioning.ts` now generates a `provRequestId` (format `prov-<8 hex>`) per provisioning attempt and all 6 internal step-failure returns (slug reserve, template copy, DB open + admin create, uploads dir, DNS record, activate) now return the same message: `Signup failed. Please try again or contact support with reference <id>.` The reference is included in the matching `logger.error` entry so ops can correlate user complaints with the exact step that broke. Input-validation errors (email, slug taken/invalid, plan) still return specific user-actionable messages — only the infra-level step failures are collapsed. (trace-signup-004)

- [x] PROD97 + PROD98. **PM2 config audit + graceful shutdown handlers — both already satisfied, no code changes required.** Audit of `ecosystem.config.js` confirms: no hardcoded absolute paths (`cwd` + `out_file` + `error_file` all built from `path.join(root, ...)` with `root = __dirname`), no hardcoded IPs, env values read from project-root `.env` via `parseDotEnv()` helper, log files land under `./logs/` relative to repo root. Entries already present for `wait_ready`, `listen_timeout`, `kill_timeout`, `max_memory_restart`, `merge_logs`. `packages/server/src/index.ts` already has a full graceful shutdown routine at lines 3027–3102: `shutdown(signal)` closes the HTTP listener, cancels every tracked `setInterval` via `backgroundIntervals`, stops the WebSocket heartbeat via `stopWebSocketHeartbeat()`, closes the tenant pool via `closeAllTenantDbs()`, closes master + single-tenant DBs, shuts down the worker pool via `shutdownWorkerPool()`, and force-exits after 10s if anything hangs. Wired to `SIGTERM` + `SIGINT` plus `uncaughtException` + `unhandledRejection` via `handleFatal()` (exit code 1 for fatal, 0 for clean). Server typecheck clean (`npx tsc --noEmit`). (PROD97, PROD98)
